Normally, the pilot or copilot controls elevator trim with the electric elevator trim switches and a trim disconnect switch on the pilot and copilot control wheels.  However, elevator trim can also be controlled manually using the elevator trim wheel.  The elevator trim tab is a little different from other trim tabs.  It incorporates an anti-servo action.  That is, as the elevator is displaced from the neutral position, the trim tab moves in the same direction as the applied control surface.  This increases the effective control surface area and the manual force required to further deflect the elevator. Normally, the pilot or copilot controls elevator trim with the electric elevator trim switches and a trim disconnect switch on the pilot and copilot control wheels.  However, elevator trim can also be controlled manually using the elevator trim wheel.  The elevator trim tab is a little different from other trim tabs.  It incorporates an anti-servo action.  That is, as the elevator is displaced from the neutral position, the trim tab moves in the same direction as the applied control surface.  This increases the effective control surface area and the manual force required to further deflect the elevator.
